2023 will include almost all of the employees affected by the announcement. We expect most of those affected will no longer be reflected in our headcount by the end of the second quarter of 2023, subject to local law and consultation requirements.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We also announced actions to optimize our global office space and our expectation that we would incur exit costs relating to office space reductions of approximately $0.5 billion in the first quarter of 2023. We may incur additional charges in the future as we further evaluate our real estate needs.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In January 2023 we</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> completed an assessment of the useful lives of our servers and network equipment, resulting in a change in the estimated useful life of our servers and certain network equipment to six years. For assets in service as of December 31, 2022, we expect that the effect of this change will be a reduction of depreciation expense of approximately $3.4 billion for the full fiscal year 2023. We will disclose the effect of the change on our depreciation expense, net income, and earnings per share in our quarterly and annual fiscal year 2023 reporting.</font></div><div id="ieabf13aee49d4e72822b745f674459c8_46"></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">iii.</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:6.92pt">Change in the segment reporting of DeepMind</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In our fourth quarter earnings release, we announced that beginning in the first quarter of 2023, DeepMind, previously reported within Other Bets, will be reported as part of Alphabet's unallocated corporate costs reflecting its increasing collaboration with Google Services, Google Cloud, and Other Bets.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Today we further announced that we are bringing together part of Google Research (the Brain Team) and DeepMind to significantly accelerate our progress in AI. This change will not affect first quarter reporting. The group, called Google DeepMind, will be reported in Alphabet&#8217;s unallocated corporate costs beginning in the second quarter of 2023.</font></div><div style="height:45pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:45pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Two additional changes effective beginning in the first quarter of 2023&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">iv.</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:6.9pt">Changes in segment cost allocations</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Beginning in the first quarter of 2023, we updated and simplified our cost allocation methodologies to provide our business leaders with increased transparency for decision-making. For example&#58; (i) certain costs associated with corporate initiatives supporting consumer-facing activities, previously reflected in unallocated corporate costs, are now allocated to Google Services&#59; and (ii) centrally-managed shared research and development activities, including our shared developer tools, are now allocated based on an updated measure of the relative benefit derived from the services. </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As a result of these changes, more of the previously unallocated corporate costs are allocated to our segments, and more of certain previously allocated costs are allocated to our consumer-facing Google Services products and less to Google Cloud enterprise products.</font></div><div id="ieabf13aee49d4e72822b745f674459c8_61"></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">v.</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;padding-left:9.67pt">Timing of our annual employee equity grants</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the second quarter of 2022 we informed our employees that, beginning in 2023, the timing of our annual employee stock-based compensation awards would shift from January to March. While the shift in timing itself will not affect the amount of stock-based compensation expense over the full f</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">iscal year 2023</font><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, it results in relatively less expense recognized in the first quarter compared to the remaining quarters of the year.</font></div><div id="ieabf13aee49d4e72822b745f674459c8_342"></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Recast historical segment results</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">After the segment reporting changes noted in items (iii) and (iv) above, unallocated corporate costs primarily include AI-focused shared R&#38;D activities&#59; corporate initiatives such as our philanthropic activities&#59; and corporate shared costs such as finance, certain human resource costs, and legal, including certain fines and settlements. In the first quarter of 2023, unallocated corporate costs will also include charges associated with reductions in our workforce and office space. Additionally, hedging gains (losses) related to revenue continue to be included in unallocated corporate costs.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#3c4043;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In our Q1 reported results, you will see that prior periods have been recast to reflect the revised segment presentation of DeepMind and the cost allocation changes, respectively items (iii) and (iv) above. </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;padding-left:18pt;text-align:justify"><font
